The O
Ayalon I-LOC
Cave I-LOC
is O
a O
large O
underground O

located O
near O
Ramla I-LOC
, O
Israel I-LOC
. O

The O
cave O
, O
300 O
feet O
deep O
, O
with O

branch O
extends O
almost O
2.5 O
kilometres O

the O

in O
Israel I-LOC
. O

Researchers O
announced O
that O

have O
so O
far O
discovered O
eight O
new O
species O
, O
all O
without O

four O

and O
four O

unknown O
to O
science O
. O

They O

two O

species O
and O
two O

species O
, O

that O
this O

might O
help O
better O
understand O

water O

of O
the O
region O
. O

cave O
was O
first O

when O
a O
small O
opening O
was O
discerned O
in O

. O

to O

is O
unique O

that O

thick O

. O

The O

will O

to O
the O
public O

. O

As O

cave O
was O
completely O
cut O

from O
the O

environment O

sustained O
an O
independent O
